  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_44b5cb12-ddeb-4edf-86e1-89fd4ca4addd'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer10982484612030993779"><b>BEWARE:<br/>LETHALLY SEDUCTIVE ALPHA MALE OF IMMENSE STRENGTH AND DARK EROTICISM. DO NOT LOOK AT HIM. DO NOT TOUCH HIM. DO NOT BE TEMPTED.   <span id="freeText10982484612030993779" style="display:none"><b>BEWARE:<br />LETHALLY SEDUCTIVE ALPHA MALE OF IMMENSE STRENGTH AND DARK EROTICISM. DO NOT LOOK AT HIM. DO NOT TOUCH HIM. DO NOT BE TEMPTED. DO NOT BE <i>SEDUCED</i>....</b><br /><br />With his long, black hair and dark, mesmerising eyes, Adam Black is Trouble with a capital T. Immortal, arrogant, and intensly sensual, he is free to roam across time and continents in pursuit of his insatiable desires. That is, until a curse strips him of his immortality and makes him invisible, a cruel fate for so irresistible a man. Now Adam's only hope for survival is in the hands of the one woman who can actually see him.<br /><br />Enter law student Gabrielle O'Callaghan. For Gabrielle, cursed with the ability to see both worlds, Mortal and Faery, it is the beginning of a long, dangerous seduction. But as Adam's quest to regain his immortality plunges them into a world of timeless magic, the price of surrender could be their very lives. Unless they can thwart the cosnpiracy that threatens both Mortal and Faery realms...and give them a shot at a destiny few mortals ever know: glorious, wondrous, endless love...</span>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1168530-does-this-series-need-to-be-read-in-order">Does this series need to be read in order? The Fever Series definitely did. Thanks in advance.</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1168530'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F112752.The_Immortal_Highlander">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/1168530-does-this-series-need-to-be-read-in-order">3 years ago</a>
</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionPermalink'>
<a href="/questions/1168530-does-this-series-need-to-be-read-in-order">Add your answer</a>
</li>
</ul>
</div>

</div>
<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/21713684-tanya"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1523646213i/21713684._UX100_CR0,13,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/21713684-tanya">Tanya</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The answer is mostly no. It's nice to read them in order because there are characters that appear in more than one book--Adam Black, for example---but<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The answer is mostly no. It's nice to read them in order because there are characters that appear in more than one book--Adam Black, for example---but it doesn't necessarily affect your understanding of a story when such a character re-appears. Enough information is given about the character so you know where he fits. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer378931629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16623171119044718245">The Immortal Highlander was another 5+ instalment from the Highlander series :) Karen Marie Moning just keeps getting better and better with every book :)<br/><br/>I've read the first one and didn't like it much, but in a way I'm glad because Adam Black first appeared in that one :) Although, I have to say, he was pretty bad in the beginning, I would never have thought he'd get his own book, he was like the bad guy :O But boy am I glad he did <3<br/><br/>In the previous book Adam sacrifices a part of his life force</span>
  <span id="freeText16623171119044718245" style="display:none">The Immortal Highlander was another 5+ instalment from the Highlander series :) Karen Marie Moning just keeps getting better and better with every book :)<br><br>I've read the first one and didn't like it much, but in a way I'm glad because Adam Black first appeared in that one :) Although, I have to say, he was pretty bad in the beginning, I would never have thought he'd get his own book, he was like the bad guy :O But boy am I glad he did &lt;3<br><br>In the previous book Adam sacrifices a part of his life force to save Dageus's life, and for that he is punished by his queen. She sent him to the human world, turned him into a human, and on top of that, he became invisible to everyone. Poor guy. Gabrielle is a decendant of people who are able to see the Faery, and she lives in constant fear of being discovered. One day she stumbles upon Adam, and she's unable to resist his good looks (it's actually seriously fan-fucking-tastic, mesmerising, panties-melting, gorgeus, seductive, perfect looks) and he begins stalking her as she is the only one that can see him. <br><br><br>Adam and Gabby were really great! He is pretty used to his awsomeness, he actually expects ever woman to fall at his feet because he knows he is irresistible. That, of course, doesn't happen with Gabrielle (oh yeah you go girl!). The first time they meet she runs away, than she kicks him in the head XD That was funny hahah, and Adam can't believe she's not falling for him. So he, of course again, decides to seduce her XD They had their happy moments, but i'm kinda upset the first sex took so long to happen :PPP But oh well XD Drustan and Dageus appeared in this one, oh how I loved that part &lt;3 &lt;3 And one of the best scenes is when they see Adam hahahahahah that was great :)<br><br>The ending - wow the ending was just perfect! One of the best epilogues ever, I cried like a baby <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/?action=view&amp;current=815594.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a> It was just beautiful, what Adam did and how it all turned out <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/?action=view&amp;current=836920.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374025ra/727915.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Considering they all get more perfect, more sexual and more seductive with each book, I'm afraid to continue reading lol, this will give me a complex XDXD</span>

<div id="review_47595317" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/47595317" />
    <a title="Dina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1918270-dina"><img alt="Dina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460302951p2/1918270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/47595317?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer47595317" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10145041743408762994">Damn, it's good to be Adam Black - sorry, I couldn't resist, LOL - but I bet it's better to be Adam Black's lover!<br/><br/>Adam is one of those heroes you just love to hate - or hate to love, either way works for me. He was selfish, arrogant, manipulative and didn't have any qualms about using anyone and anything to his own advantage. He was also as handome and sexy as one can be, which only helped him to get what he wanted. BUT there was <i>something</i> beneath all that, something that shouldn't be there cons</span>
  <span id="freeText10145041743408762994" style="display:none">Damn, it's good to be Adam Black - sorry, I couldn't resist, LOL - but I bet it's better to be Adam Black's lover!<br /><br />Adam is one of those heroes you just love to hate - or hate to love, either way works for me. He was selfish, arrogant, manipulative and didn't have any qualms about using anyone and anything to his own advantage. He was also as handome and sexy as one can be, which only helped him to get what he wanted. BUT there was <i>something</i> beneath all that, something that shouldn't be there considering he was basically a soulless and unfeeling <i>Fae</i>. Had it always been there? I really didn't see it in the previous book in the series, and I think KMM has done a great job making me believe in Adam's "change of heart" - figuratively speaking, since <i>Faes</i> don't have hearts.<br /><br />Gabby was funny and likeable, but not really remarkable. I think the "problem" was, Adam stole the show and she didn't have enough "spark" to stand on her own. Bottom line, she wasn't as interesting as Lisa, Gwen and Chloe, the heroines in the previous books. BTW, Gwen, Chloe and their respective MacKeltar husbands - sighs! - make more than an simple appearance and play important roles in <b>The Immortal Highlander</b>. I have to say, their reactions when they see Adam "in the flesh" for the first time was priceless, LOL. I had expected to see Circenn too - after all, he was Adam's son - but he was a no-show. Oh well, we can't always have it all, right?<br /><br />Once again, KMM told a story that kept me captivated and entertained. The love scenes were hot - not hard to imagine, since Adam oozed sex appeal - and there was always something happening to keep me turning the pages anxiously. Aoibheal's revelation after she restored Adam's immortality was unexpected and I had a hard time buying it. I really didn't see how he could have been fooled like that. Anyway, that wasn't enough to ruin the story for me.<br /><br />This book was nicely tied to the previous ones in the series - I particularly liked how Adam made everything "right" for Circenn and Lisa, the H/h in <b>The Highlander's Touch</b> -, so this is one series that definitely <i>must</i> be read in order.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10145041743408762994" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10025399683258248045" style="display:none"><i>Written June 25, 2015</i><br><br><b>4 1/2 Stars - Simply wonderful in the very best kind of 'Highlander' style</b><br><br><i>The Immortal Highlander</i> is a contemporary (slightly) paranormal 'Highlander' romance. I listened to the 10 hrs audiobook excellent narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/521640.Phil_Gigante" title="Phil Gigante" rel="nofollow noopener">Phil Gigante</a>. <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/image.jpg1_zpsv3vhyk5b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>Yay, I love these Scottish men...</b><br>Once again a great installment in a wonderful humorous, romantic hot, very well-written series. <br><br>*********************************************<br><br><i>Present day in U.S.</i><br><br>The immortal Prince Faery <b>Adam Black</b> is punished by his, right now angry, mighty queen. The evil penalty is that he for a time is an invisible mortal man. He travels from Scotland to U.S where he by a coincidence meets the law student <b>Gabrielle O'Callaghan</b>. Gabrielle is cursed with the ability to see both worlds, Mortal and Faery, and Adam needs her. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/47525e40-84d8-4046-93e8-a2a05e0f9ef8_zpstdtxhg0m.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430846309i/14769075.jpg" alt=" photo 47525e40-84d8-4046-93e8-a2a05e0f9ef8_zpstdtxhg0m.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“For the record, Irish,” he informed her tightly, just in case she got the wrong idea, “I kneel to no one.” <br><br>. . . . . <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Cartoon/Couple%20drawings/d7bcae63-45ff-4e58-8c85-cfc0045c4d62_zpsoyclhqz7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435252194i/15322019.jpg" alt=" photo d7bcae63-45ff-4e58-8c85-cfc0045c4d62_zpsoyclhqz7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/47525e40-84d8-4046-93e8-a2a05e0f9ef8_zpstdtxhg0m.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430846309i/14769075.jpg" alt=" photo 47525e40-84d8-4046-93e8-a2a05e0f9ef8_zpstdtxhg0m.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>Amusing, romantic, steamy and just great</b><br>This was the third for me in this "time-travel" series (loved part <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/520477320" rel="nofollow noopener">#4 ★★★★★</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/521362522?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">#5 ★★★★☆</a>). It seems to be one book a year for me but it's always good to be back in this wonderful <i>Highlander</i> land again. This über sexy caveman hero, Adam Black, turned out to be amazing fun to know already in the first chapter. He "made" this story, as these male highlanders always are the yummy icing on the cake in this amusing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/48206.Karen_Marie_Moning" title="Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">Karen Marie Moning</a> world. ~ Precisely nothing to complain about, just marvelous enjoying.<br><br>The narrator did it well too. I like his voice a lot (for the male characters anyway). ~ It will be more books / audiobooks in this series and I'll not wait another year.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>I LIKE - men like Adam... **drool**</b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/147050846?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tatiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tatiana" href="/user/show/2250020-tatiana">Tatiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781423341628" href="/book/show/10360980-immortal-highlander-the">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250020-tatiana?shelf=romancelandia">romancelandia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer147050846" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8573261005928300744">So, I was trying to ease my <i>Fever</i> withdrawal pains by reading one of Moning's Highlander romances. Pretty much had to drop it after 15 minutes of listening to it. I should have known it wouldn't work for me after hearing this, right at the beginning:<br/><br/><i>Adam Black:<br/><br/>Tuatha De Danaan, a rogue even among his own kind. His favored glamour is that of an intensely sexual Highland blacksmith with a powerful rippling body, golden skin, long black hair, mesmerizing eyes. Highly intelligent, lethally seductive</i></span>
  <span id="freeText8573261005928300744" style="display:none">So, I was trying to ease my <i>Fever</i> withdrawal pains by reading one of Moning's Highlander romances. Pretty much had to drop it after 15 minutes of listening to it. I should have known it wouldn't work for me after hearing this, right at the beginning:<br /><br /><i>Adam Black:<br /><br />Tuatha De Danaan, a rogue even among his own kind. His favored glamour is that of an intensely sexual Highland blacksmith with a powerful rippling body, golden skin, long black hair, mesmerizing eyes. Highly intelligent, lethally seductive...<br /><br /><br />- from the O'Callaghan Books of the Fae, London</i><br /><br />So, Adam is some powerful fae and all he cares about is looking like a sexy <b>blacksmith</b> with long hair? Just couldn't take this seriously. Can you blame me?<br /><br />Goodness, I miss Jericho!<br /><br />P.S. Men should not narrate romance audiobooks IMO. It's creepy.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8573261005928300744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3436142528" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3436142528" />
    <a title="Anna *Bran. San. Stan*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/98245866-anna-bran-san-stan"><img alt="Anna *Bran. San. Stan*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593184464p2/98245866.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3436142528?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna *Bran. San. Stan*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna *Bran. San. Stan*" href="/user/show/98245866-anna-bran-san-stan">Anna *Bran. San. Stan*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/98245866-anna-bran-san-stan?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/98245866-anna-bran-san-stan?shelf=have-or-will-reread">have-or-will-reread</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3436142528" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17741749383655332384"><b>Adam Black is no longer immortal! <i>"[He] had been killing time since – endeavoring grimly to ignore that, for the first time in his timeless existence, time was returning the favor."</i><br/>All the hearts ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️ and stars ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️ for Adam Black’s story!</b> Why did I wait for so long to continue this series?!<br/><br/><b>Reasons why this book is amazing:</b><br/>✅ <u>Adam Black</u>: mischievous, hotter than hell, several-thousand-year-old immortal Tuatha Dé (Fae) turned human<br/>✅ finally: a <u>Sidhe-seer</u> (Fae-seer) and our heroine at t</span>
  <span id="freeText17741749383655332384" style="display:none"><b>Adam Black is no longer immortal! <i>"[He] had been killing time since – endeavoring grimly to ignore that, for the first time in his timeless existence, time was returning the favor."</i><br />All the hearts ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️ and stars ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️ for Adam Black’s story!</b> Why did I wait for so long to continue this series?!<br /><br /><b>Reasons why this book is amazing:</b><br />✅ <u>Adam Black</u>: mischievous, hotter than hell, several-thousand-year-old immortal Tuatha Dé (Fae) turned human<br />✅ finally: a <u>Sidhe-seer</u> (Fae-seer) and our heroine at that! (cf. Fever series)<br />✅ the <u>humorous, tongue-in-cheek tone</u> I missed in <i>The Dark Highlander</i> is back (see below for some samples)<br />✅ <u>steamy sex</u>, not overdone (disclaimer: adult content, 18+!)<br /><br />The <b>ties to the other books</b> in this series and the Fever series make this book even more amazing:<br />✅ Drustan and Dageus <u>McKeltar</u>, Gwen and Chloe<br />✅ <u>Darroc</u>’s history<br />✅ <u>Circenn</u>, Adam's son (though I would have liked for him and his family to actually make an appearance)<br />✅ Adam’s history with <u>Morganna</u> (Circenn’s mother)<br />✅ more <u>world-building</u> in preparation for Fever<br /><br />I’ve said it in my reviews of the previous books and I’ll say it again: READ THIS SERIES! If you’ve loved the Fever series or if you like <b>feel-good, tongue-in-cheek, humorous romance</b> (with a touch of historical fiction and fantasy) in general, you will be in for a fun reading experience; even if you didn’t much like the first book (I didn’t either), it’s really worth hanging in there.<br /><br /><u>Books in this series so far:</u><br /><i>Beyond the Highland Mist: ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br />To Tame a Highland Warrior ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br />The Highlander‘s Touch ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3237665041?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of the Highlander</a> ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3432578864" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Highlander</a> ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3436142528?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Highlander</a> ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️<br /><br /></i>Here are some <b>samples of Moning’s tongue-in-cheek writing</b> I love so much:<br /><br /><u>Adam’s musings on the significance of time:</u><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“[Adam had] become obsessed with increments of time. It was an embarrassingly mortal affliction. Next thing he knew, he’d be wearing a watch.”<br /><br />“Upon arriving in Cincinnati, [Adam had] found Circenn’s residence vacant, and had no idea where to look for him next. He’d taken up residence there himself, and <b>had been killing time since – endeavoring grimly to ignore that, for the first time in his timeless existence, time was returning the favor</b> – waiting for Circenn to return.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><u>Gabby on the impact of simple decisions such as buying a cup of coffee:</u><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Later Gabby would realize that it was all the cup of coffee’s fault. Every awful thing that happened to her from that moment on could be traced directly back to that cup of coffee with the <b>stunning simplicity of an airtight conditional argument:</b> If not for A (said cup of coffee), then not B (blowing job interview), hence not C (having to go into work that night), and certainly not D (the horrible thing that happened to her there) . . . on to infinity.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><u>Adam’s experience with being a human male:</u><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“It had just been made excruciatingly clear to him that the human male brain and the human male cock couldn’t both sustain sufficient amounts of blood to function at the same time. It was one or the other, and the human male apparently didn’t get to choose which one.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><u>Adam on semantics:</u><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Gabby nodded. ‘I have one of the, er . . . fairies here with me –‘<br />‘Tuatha Dé,’ Adam corrected irritably. ‘You’re bloody well making me sound like Tinkerbell.’”</i>
</blockquote><br />___________________________________<br />Just one errant thought: Why is everyone in this series a frigging virgin??</span>
  <a data-text-id="17741749383655332384" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1848412391" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1848412391" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1848412391?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>

        rated it

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=immortals">immortals</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=timetravel">timetravel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=4fantasy-lovestories">4fantasy-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=dimensiontravel-paralleluniverse">dimensiontravel-paralleluniverse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=fairies-fae-pixies">fairies-fae-pixies</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1848412391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16590801041196299745">Adam Black has piqued my curiosity in the previous Highlander books: A larger than life Fae, a Tuatha De, arrogant, sparkly beautiful, seductive, unpredictable, sexual, a player, Queen’s consort. A manipulative, totally dark in soul and his thinking male. <br/>He loves playing with the humans’ lives, plotting and pretending being God.<br/><br/>Gabrielle "Gabby" O’Callaghan is a Sidhe-seer and she has the ability to see both worlds; mortal and faery (once again I wish I had read this series before Fever...).<br/>Gab</span>
  <span id="freeText16590801041196299745" style="display:none">Adam Black has piqued my curiosity in the previous Highlander books: A larger than life Fae, a Tuatha De, arrogant, sparkly beautiful, seductive, unpredictable, sexual, a player, Queen’s consort. A manipulative, totally dark in soul and his thinking male. <br />He loves playing with the humans’ lives, plotting and pretending being God.<br /><br />Gabrielle "Gabby" O’Callaghan is a Sidhe-seer and she has the ability to see both worlds; mortal and faery (once again I wish I had read this series before Fever...).<br />Gabby is trying very hard to live a normal life. She is a law student working for a law company that she hates. She also pretends that she does not see fairies. This is something that her grandmother taught her…because fairies are manipulative, soulless, and incapable of feeling anything. They are bad bad beings. <br /><br />It does not matter that Gabby since she was a kid loved them and was fantasizing that a fae prince would come and sweep her off her feet. Her grandmother was strict “Avoid them with any cost. When they find out about you, RUN!”<br /><br />And then Gabby meets the worst of them all. <br />Adam’s life collides with her life, when she lifts her eyes and sees him and her glance stays there. She does not pretend that she does not see him or that he is transparent and she is looking something behind him. She cannot take her eyes from him. And then she RUNS. And he RUNS after her. Of course she will be caught LOL<br /><br />Trying to survive a terrible curse, Adam will use Gabby. They will travel from USA to Scotland, attempting to avoid other fairies and Hunters and not be killed in the process. Our favorite highlanders and druids Drustan and Dageus will help. <br /><br />In the end Adam has to make decisions. How far can he go? How many things he can sacrifice for Gabby? How can he fall in love, when he is not supposed to feel anything.<br /><br />This is by far my favorite book in the series. Adam is definitely my favorite character.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16590801041196299745" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/177568225?book_show_action=true">Jun 17, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6295261-the-immortal-highlander">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-hero">favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=scrumptious-hero">scrumptious-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=dark-hero">dark-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer177568225" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13380279421308077001">Huge 5+ stars<br/><br/>Wow! Just Wow! I adore this book. Adore it! By far my favorite of the series. <br/><br/>Adam Black *dreamy sigh* is an immortal dark Fae prince with an abundance of mischievousness, arrogance, dangerous unpredictability, and a devilish insatiable sexuality. He's the ultimate seducer. The story begins with Adam being punished by the Faery Queen (who adores him, of course) for his repeated interference with his "toy" humans. She strips him of his immortality and makes him invisible to all aroun</span>
  <span id="freeText13380279421308077001" style="display:none">Huge 5+ stars<br /><br />Wow! Just Wow! I adore this book. Adore it! By far my favorite of the series. <br /><br />Adam Black *dreamy sigh* is an immortal dark Fae prince with an abundance of mischievousness, arrogance, dangerous unpredictability, and a devilish insatiable sexuality. He's the ultimate seducer. The story begins with Adam being punished by the Faery Queen (who adores him, of course) for his repeated interference with his "toy" humans. She strips him of his immortality and makes him invisible to all around him. Such a plight and pity for our poor irresistible Adam. <br /><br />Enter law student Gabrielle "Gabby" O’Callaghan. Gabby, a Sidhe-seer, has the ability to see both worlds; mortal and faery. From the moment she lays eyes on Adam, she knows he could be her undoing, which is very dangerous for her, as the Tuatha De, which Adam is a member, have eradicated all Sidhe-seers from the earth. <br /><br />Thus begins a long and dangerous seduction that will ultimately changes both their lives forever. Regardless of how how hard she tries, Gabby can't seem to avoid Adam, he everywhere. Invisible to all but her, he pampers and treats her in way she's not accustom and relentlessly temps her with the promise of erotic pleasure. Pretty temping for a lonely virgin, I'd say. Unfortunately, danger intrudes on this sensual pursuit and Adam’s quest to regain his immortality immerses them into the deadly politics of the Tuatha De.<br /><br />Adam is by far my favorite character of the series. I could tell KMM had a blast writing him. In fact, Adam kinda steals the show, so to speak, almost to the detriment of the other characters. As much as I love Gabby and feel she's a strong and wonderful heroine, she does pale and become somewhat overshadowed by Adam's bigger than life character. <br /><br /><i>The Immortal Highlander</i> is a fast paced read, that not only provides laugh out loud moment but also is an extremely sensual and erotic read. This is a book I will read again and again and again. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13380279421308077001" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer708740661974552105"><br/><b>5 Swoonworthy Stars!! I am <i>Given</i>.</b> My soul is yours Adam Black! Another fantastic installment in this series, this one rounding out not only Adam’s story, but the MacKeltars too!! <br/><br/>Poor Adam is being punished for doing something good, but because of his meddling in the human world, he’s been rendered powerless in his own. The prince is no more; he’s just a mere mortal wandering aimlessly unbeknownst even to his own kind. That is until he crosses paths with Gabrielle O'Callaghan who has a gift, or </span>
  <span id="freeText708740661974552105" style="display:none"><br /><b>5 Swoonworthy Stars!! I am <i>Given</i>.</b> My soul is yours Adam Black! Another fantastic installment in this series, this one rounding out not only Adam’s story, but the MacKeltars too!! <br /><br />Poor Adam is being punished for doing something good, but because of his meddling in the human world, he’s been rendered powerless in his own. The prince is no more; he’s just a mere mortal wandering aimlessly unbeknownst even to his own kind. That is until he crosses paths with Gabrielle O'Callaghan who has a gift, or in her mind a curse, and is able to see the Fae! He is the only fairy that Gabby has ever made eye contact with and it changes her life forever and his is just about to begin!<br /><br />Adam, Adam, Adam…oh my, my you <b>cocky, sexy, naughty, brawny, wicked boy!! RAWRRRR!!</b> Gabby is feisty, strong, smart, beautiful, and very lonely, my heart broke for her. She needs a man like Adam in her life; even though he and the possibility of a relationship with him go against everything she’s been taught. The two of them can’t deny the overwhelming desire they have for one another and as they journey together to bring Adam back to his world, they start to fall in love. <br /><br />This book was fabulous. It was funny, passionate, heartbreaking, heartwarming and loaded with testosterone!! <b> WOW!!!</b> The MacKeltars and Adam had my heart a flutter and I was quivering and quaking! The sisterhood that develops between Gabby, Gwen and Chloe was lovely. Although the books that I’ve read in this series followed somewhat of a formula, the characters and the storyline is what sets them apart. Each one leaves you with a satisfying ending, <b>BUT</b> this one nearly brought me to my knees!! My heart pounded, I was breathless and teary-eyed when I read this beautiful, emotional ending and epilogue, and then went back and read it again and again!! <br /><br />I can’t recommend this book, and the two that came before, enough. Once again I thank my lovely friend Kristen for showing me the way to these books that now sit proudly on my favorites shelf!! <br /><br />This could be Adam and Gabby’s song:<br /><i> Crashed</i> by Daughtry<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E5uArjOj5fk">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E5uArj...</a><br /><br />From your face, your eyes<br />are burning into me<br />You saved me, you gave me<br />Just what I need<br />ohh, just what I need<br /><br />And then I crashed into you<br />and I went up in flames<br />Could've been the death of me<br />But then you breathed your breath in me<br />Then I crashed into you<br />like a runaway train<br />You will consume me<br />But, I can't walk away<br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3209146-sam-s2-im-made-of-awesomness?shelf=fiery">fiery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3209146-sam-s2-im-made-of-awesomness?shelf=highlanders">highlanders</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3209146-sam-s2-im-made-of-awesomness?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3209146-sam-s2-im-made-of-awesomness?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146157512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14554045056921014696">SEE THIS REVIEW AT <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2011/08/immortal-highlander-karen-marie-moning.html'>http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a> AND THEN BECOME A FOLLOWER!!<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Damn, its good to be me.<br/>-	Adam Black, on being Adam Black</i>
</b><br/><br/>Adam Black is a Tuatha De’Danaan, rouge even among his own kind. His favoured glamour is that of an intensely sexual Highland blacksmith with a powerful rippling body, golden skin, long black hair, and dark, mesmerizing eyes. Highly intelligent and lethally seductive. Alleged to have nearly broken The Compact on not one, but two occasions. He is, by</span>
  <span id="freeText14554045056921014696" style="display:none">SEE THIS REVIEW AT <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2011/08/immortal-highlander-karen-marie-moning.html">http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a> AND THEN BECOME A FOLLOWER!!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Damn, its good to be me.<br />-	Adam Black, on being Adam Black</i>
</b><br /><br />Adam Black is a Tuatha De’Danaan, rouge even among his own kind. His favoured glamour is that of an intensely sexual Highland blacksmith with a powerful rippling body, golden skin, long black hair, and dark, mesmerizing eyes. Highly intelligent and lethally seductive. Alleged to have nearly broken The Compact on not one, but two occasions. He is, by far, the most dangerous and unpredictable of his race.<br /><br />Oh and did I mention frigging hot to trot with a shlong the size of King Kong!?!?!?!? Oh *sighs dreamily* Adam Black, sex is not the answer. Sex is the question. Yes is my answer – YES! I can only imagine that if I ever got my hands onto your fairy body the sex would be so good that even the neighbours would need to have a cigarette.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>The other day upon the stair, I saw a man who wasn’t there. He wasn’t there again today; how I wish he’d go away! <br />-	Gabrielle O’Callaghan, on Adam Black. </i>
</b><br /><br />I enjoyed Gabrielle’s character. I do tend to get a bit pissy at female characters with their constant self analysis about crap that is totally irrelevant. Not that Gabrielle wasn’t completely without a little self deprecation; it was just that it wasn’t to the extent where I felt like clobbering her one over the head with a mallet. She was intelligent – studying to be a lawyer in fact. And she withstood Adams sexy charms longer than any sane woman would have. I bow to her.<br /><br />So needless to say, I loved this book. This of course is the story of Adam Black and Gabrielle O’Callaghan and is easily the best I have read so far in this series. I found there was a lot of laugh out loud moments is the book. The plot was enthralling and fast paced. Adam *sigh* is being punished by his Queen for restoring the life of Daegus Mackelter and has forced him into being human and invisible to everyone around him. That is, everyone except Gabby. Gabrielle is a sidhe-seer (someone who can see the Fae). When Adam realized that she can see him, he sets out ruthlessly to get Gabrielle to help him set his life back to rights. Gabrielle has grown up thinking that all fairies are evil so is very wary about helping Adam, but learns quickly along the way that you should never take anything at face value.<br /><br />Of course there are the usual baddies who are set out to release Hunters into the human world and kill Adam Black.<br /><br />The romance between Adam and Gabrielle was palpable. They have grant banter and such a great attraction toward one another. Gabrielle withstood Adams charms for an awfully long time and <i>just</i> when you think something was finally going to happen – they get ....interrupted. KMM made these two characters work for each other, with Adam perpetually trying to seduce Gabrielle.<br /><br />Faults? I am a little over the all the mid twenty year old virgins. Can we not have just one girl in the series that already had her ‘maidenhead’ taken by say, I don’t know....the jerk down the road? And one more tiny thing, long hair down to ones waist, would be so terribly disgusting on a man. Can you imagine the knots? Bleh...<br /><br />Summary – The Immortal Highlander was a truly wonderful read. I haven’t laughed out loud in a book like this for a long time. I recommend this to anyone hasn’t read it.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16710067756752580863"><b>★★★★4.75 Stars !★★★★ </b> <br/><br/>Would highly recommend ! I'm so in love with series x<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477589463i/20969368._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>

  <span id="freeText10925765701971448604" style="display:none">I can't believe that I had never read a KMM book before I started this series....I must have been on another planet ;)<br /><br />This was another fantastic addition to the Highlander series. <span id="freeTextContainer17185013192350149187">Adam Black, is part of the <i>Tuatha De Danaan</i> who are an advanced race of immortals. They are also known as Faes or fairies, but Adam is no <i>Tinkerbell</i>. He's arrogant, unpredictable, unbelievably sexy and can seduce anyone that carries the X chromosome.<br/><br/><i>"He had a come-and-get-me-baby-I'm-pure-trouble-and-you're-gonna-love-it kind of attitude."</i><br/><br/>He's so sexy, he makes me want to growl, GRRRRRRR! ;)<br/><br/>Aiobheal the Queen of the <i>Tuatha De's</i> punishes Adam for his interference in the world of mortals. She stri</span>
  <span id="freeText17185013192350149187" style="display:none">Adam Black, is part of the <i>Tuatha De Danaan</i> who are an advanced race of immortals. They are also known as Faes or fairies, but Adam is no <i>Tinkerbell</i>. He's arrogant, unpredictable, unbelievably sexy and can seduce anyone that carries the X chromosome.<br /><br /><i>"He had a come-and-get-me-baby-I'm-pure-trouble-and-you're-gonna-love-it kind of attitude."</i><br /><br />He's so sexy, he makes me want to growl, GRRRRRRR! ;)<br /><br />Aiobheal the Queen of the <i>Tuatha De's</i> punishes Adam for his interference in the world of mortals. She strips him of immortality and powers. To make it worse she also curses him with the <i>feth fiada</i> which makes him invisible to mankind. No one can hear, see or touch him. Until he stumbles upon Gabrielle.<br /><br />Gabrielle, is intelligent and has the gift of sight which enables her to see him and any other Faeries walking the mortal earth. Adam discovers her secret of being capable of communicating with him, and pursues her constantly and tries to break down her resolve by trying to seduce her. <br /><br /><i>Hunger for me, ka-lyrra, he thought silently, get addicted to me. I will be both venom and antidote, your poison and your only cure.</i><br /><br />Adam needs to persuade Gabby in helping him restore his powers and immortality. This is where KMM, takes us on another wonderful trip of time travel, romance, magic and just flat out fun! Loved it! <br /><br /></span>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398732i/770873._SX540_.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If I swoon any further from this series I would just melt into the floor/pavement/W.E. Although I didn't get enough of my favorite Kilt wearers, but what I did get was Adam Black and this dole been approved. <br><br>Story resumes shortly before the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112755.The_Dark_Highlander__Highlander___5_" title="The Dark Highlander (Highlander, #5) by Karen Marie Moning" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1320434715s/112755.jpg" alt="The Dark Highlander (Highlander, #5) by Karen Marie Moning" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> end. Adam is paying the price for challenging the Queen in front of the court, by being made "human" (with all the human cravings and needs) and placed in féth fíada, therefore, invisible to human eye.<br><br>The fairies are tricky and they always think through all loop-holes, but Queen Aoibheal did count on one variable... a beautiful Sidhe-seer who can see him.<br><br>Gabrielle could see fairies since she was little, which is a dangerous thing. Sidhe-seers are hunted and kidnapped by fairies. She was to ignore and pretend like she doesn't see them as her only protection.<br><br>But when Gabrielle meets Adam... oooh wheee!!! All those years of training and self preservation fly out of the window (and I can't even blame her... come on IT'S ADAM!)<br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/Hotties/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m6sb24ibOK1qlfz9jo1_500.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398732i/770874.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Adam <s> bribes </s> coerces Gabrielle into helping him seek counsel with the Queen to acquire her pardon and get his immortality back. However, things don't go according to plan as a long time rival strikes to destroy Adam at his weakest.<br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/Emotions/?action=view&amp;current=ohnonono.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398732ra/770875.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>OK, Officially the darkest and trickiest of Fae is the hottest &amp; sweetest man! I felt so bad for him at times because I wanted to laugh at him. As a cocky (no intentional pun intended)Fae who had all the women falling over him, Gabby is frigging hilarious resisting him, especially when she meets him 2nd time around by <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ busting his lip, head-butting him and kneeing his junk.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Ouch, but so hilarious!<br><br>There are so many elements here that give a spin-off of Fever Series, that it makes me wish I read this first, but oh well!<br><br>We get to see more of the expending MacKeltar clan!<br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/Emotions/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m52kl3reyx1r9gy1p.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398732ra/770876.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u> Quote that made me want to Hug <b> KMM </b> </u><br><blockquote> <i> She understood now why her friend Elizabeth, with her near-genius, analytical mind gave wide berth to murder mysteries, psychological thrillers, and horror stories, and read only <b> romance novels </b>. Because, by God, when a woman picked up one of those steamy books, she had a firm guarantee that there would be a <b> Happily-Ever-After.</b> </i>
</blockquote>  <br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> You aren't falling for me, are you, Irish? </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/Couples/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_mcsdimW0hC1rjpl2xo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398732ra/770877.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_177879558" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/177879558" />
    <a title="Liv" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4190183-liv"><img alt="Liv" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1300208935p2/4190183.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/177879558?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liv" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liv" href="/user/show/4190183-liv">Liv</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780440334606" href="/book/show/6988761-the-immortal-highlander">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4190183-liv?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer177879558" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6064219151151534189">I am getting tired of giving a rating in between stars - I am giving this one a 2.5 stars, because similar to the Dark Highlander (this book's predecessor in the series), I thought it was more than okay but I didn't feel that I "liked" it all that much.<br/> <br/>I was very happy that Adam Black finally got a story of his own. I thought Gabrielle (or Gabby for short) was well-matched for him. In this book, we even got to see more of Drustan & Gwen, Dageus & Chloe (both couples from previous two novels in </span>
  <span id="freeText6064219151151534189" style="display:none">I am getting tired of giving a rating in between stars - I am giving this one a 2.5 stars, because similar to the Dark Highlander (this book's predecessor in the series), I thought it was more than okay but I didn't feel that I "liked" it all that much.<br /> <br />I was very happy that Adam Black finally got a story of his own. I thought Gabrielle (or Gabby for short) was well-matched for him. In this book, we even got to see more of Drustan &amp; Gwen, Dageus &amp; Chloe (both couples from previous two novels in the series) and even Darroc, one of the main villains from the author's Fever series. Overall, the story in itself was actually quite good - it had its fair share of romantic and suspense elements. However, it still failed to interest me.<br /><br />I've read KMM's Fever series first, before venturing into the Highlander series. I'm a big fan of the Fever series, but I can't say as much about the Highlander series. After having read 6 of the KMM Highlander novels, I've gotten tired of the way the stories were plotted and portrayed. Each book, although focused on a different couple as the main characters, followed a similarly predictable structure, or formula, which can be summarized as follows:<br /><br />(1) A sensual, beautiful, good-hearted, courageous woman (our female protagonist) meets a hunky, gorgeous, seductive, sexy, irristible man (our to-die-for-and-to-drool-over-for male lead). Sometimes their meeting would be a result of some time-travel plan or accident, but essentially you'd have a guy who doesn't really belong in the 21st century meet a modern-day woman.<br /><br />(2) Woman and hunky guy feel instant attraction towards each other and continue to feel horny around each other throughout the entire book.<br /><br />(3) Lady and man go through a series of flirting, teasing, seduction etc., while in the middle of some sort of trouble, mystery, or adventure. This is essentially the "mating dance" between the two lead characters. Eventually they cannot resist the urge and mutual attraction, and fall into bed together. They always have mind-blowing sex, and the lead hunk of the story always has skills that no man of our current-day standards would ever hope to match, let alone surpass. Oh, let's not forget that the lead woman (in the majority of the Highlander novels) is a virgin so her first time is well-treasured and appreciated by the man.<br /><br />(4) Lady and the said seductive man would then ensue in some sort of battle or final showdown with the villain(s) of the novel, meanwhile have more sex in between whenever and wherever possible.<br /><br />(5) Battle with the bad guys is finally won but somehow, someway the couple gets separated. The lady becomes immensely distraught with the loss of her love and goes into a state of denial, shock, deep despair.<br /><br />(6) Finally our fictional, unforgettable hunk appears again and reunites with his mate. They reconcile, have more sex, and live happily ever after. Oh, and they usually end up having babies, or plan to have babies.<br /><br />So, this just about sums up my impression of the Highlander series so far. I think you can apply the above formula to any of the first six books and you'd find that I'm really not that far off the mark.<br /><br />Really, KMM's writing style isn't bad. In fact, she has this way of writing that perfectly describes any woman's fantasy dream guy. Her romantic portrayal between the lead characters is quite well written and believable. Sometimes I can't help but sigh over the hunks in the novels. If I were to ready any one of the six books as a standalone (i.e. read only one and none of the others), each would actually earn at least a 3-star, may be even 4-star, rating in my funny accounting way. Unfortunately, I read one after another, and by the time I reached #6, I just got tired of seeing the same things again and again.<br /><br />Having said this though, I will still attempt to read book #7 of the series. After all, I've already invested so much time, I might just as well complete the journey, right? I just hope that I'll encounter something surprisingly pleasant and NEW in the next installment. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6064219151151534189" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_728256838" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728256838?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="K" class="user" itemprop="url" name="K" href="/user/show/16359109-k">K</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=arrogant-hero">arrogant-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=hero-alpha-obsessed-jealous">hero-alpha-obsessed-jealous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=love-the-hero">love-the-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=foul-mouthed-hero">foul-mouthed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728256838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8346760533905106633"><blockquote>
  <b>5+++ IMMORTAL STARS!!!!</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381071756i/4081782._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"But, second and most important, Gabby,she'd said softly,the question you must ask yourself isn't, will you get a Happily-Ever-After? The question you need to ask yourself is, will you be able to live with yourself if you don't let yourself have a happy-now, and<br/>end up having had nothing at all?</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>You were firing questions at me today, trying to get inside my head.<br/>You asked if I believed in God.<br/>I told you of course I do- I've always had a strong sense of self.<br/><br/>Your h</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8346760533905106633" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>5+++ IMMORTAL STARS!!!!</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381071756i/4081782._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"But, second and most important, Gabby,she'd said softly,the question you must ask yourself isn't, will you get a Happily-Ever-After? The question you need to ask yourself is, will you be able to live with yourself if you don't let yourself have a happy-now, and<br>end up having had nothing at all?</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>You were firing questions at me today, trying to get inside my head.<br>You asked if I believed in God.<br>I told you of course I do- I've always had a strong sense of self.<br><br>Your house is quiet now, you're sleeping upstairs and I'm alone with this blasted, idiotic book that purports to tally the sum of my life, and fact is, maybe I do. <br>But maybe, ka-lyrra, your God doesn't believe in me.</i>
</blockquote> <br><br>I don't think there was a single thing about this book that I didn't love. It was <b>mesmerizing, sexy, funny, charming, breathtaking, and utterly fantastic</b>! It kept me enthralled the entire time I was reading it. I was <i>never</i> bored. I loved all the characters, their quick wit and banter; and I can safely say this book is one of my <u>favorite paranormal romance novels</u> I've ever read. <br><br><i>My Immortal Highlander</i> is the story of <b>Gabrielle</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381074639i/4093463._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's a<b>
  <i>Sidhe-Seer</i>
</b>, or one who can see Fae. One who is taught to revile them. To never let one get close to her for they are soulless seducers who will kill you, and do it with a smile on their heartless faces.<br><br>She's <b>feisty, full of passion, Adam's Irish Ka-Lyrra, and just trying to fit into a world that she's never quite fit into</b>. She's been living her life trying to find that special guy to live it out with..but she has a secret. Even though she's supposed to be terrified of the Fae, <b>she's secretly always dreamed of one day finding her very own Fae Prince,</b> one whose icy soul she can thaw. One only she can bring into the light. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"How many times had she dreamed of doing that? Copping one tiny forbidden fairy-feel. Finally finding out if all that golden fairy skin really felt as velvety as it looked?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Then she meets <b>Adam Black</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Damn, it's good to be me." -Adam Black</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381075312i/4095979.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A <b>Fae Prince</b> who's been punished by his queen and sent to live as a human for however long she deems fit. His legend is of an <b>icy, heartless monster who should be avoided at all costs.</b> With his <b>long dark hair, dark eyes, and bands of gold around his wrists and neck</b>, he's every bit the royal Prince that Gabrielle has always dreamed of. It only he wasn't reported to be an evil seducer. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Tuatha Dé Danaan. a rogue even among his own kind His favored glamour is that of an intensely sexual<br>Highland blacksmith with a powerful rippling body, golden skin, long black hair, and dark, mesmerizing<br>eyes Highly intelligent, lethally seductive. Alleged to have nearly broken The Compact on not one. but<br>two occasions. He is, by far. the most dangerous and unpredictable of his race.<br>WARNING: EXERCISE EXTREME CAUTION IF SIGHTED.<br>AVOID CONTACT AT ALL COST.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved reading their journey and the beautiful story of how they fell in love. We have a man who <b>maybe is more than he seems</b>, and a woman who is slowly thawing the ice around his non existent soul. <i>How do you make someone love you if they don't even have a soul? A heart?</i> For such a sexy story, <b>I was very surprised on the beauty of their love.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397904i/768327.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She understood now why her friend Elizabeth, with her near-genius, analytical mind gave wide berth to<br>murder mysteries, psychological thrillers, and horror stories, and read only romance novels. Because, by God, when a woman picked up one of those steamy books, she had a firm guarantee that there would be<br>a Happily-Ever-After. That though the world outside those covers could bring such sorrow and disappointment and loneliness, between those covers, the world was a splendid place to be.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book has some moments of extreme humor as well. We get to see some of the characters from previous books make brief appearances throughout the novel. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Tell them, Gabrielle,” Adam urged impatiently.<br>Blinking, Gabby nodded. “I have one of the, er… fairies here with me –”<br>“Tuatha Dé,” Adam corrected irritably. “You’re bloody well making me sound like Tinkerbell.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381069890i/4074780.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>My advice to anyone who <i>isn't</i> interested in Paranormal Romances is to give this one a shot anyways. It may not be your topic of choice but I loved the love story so much I don't know how anyone else couldn't. <b>Give a shot.</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381073628i/4089380.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Ah, ka-lyrra, I look at you and you make me want to live a man's life with you. To wake with you and sleep with you, argue with you and make love with you, to get a silly human job and take walks in the park and live so tiny beneath such a vast sky. <br>But I will never stay with another human woman and watch her die. Never." -Adam</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>***I would recommend this novel to others***</b></span>

<div id="review_564535681" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/564535681" />
    <a title="Rae" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3580938-rae"><img alt="Rae" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425838948p2/3580938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/564535681?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rae" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rae" href="/user/show/3580938-rae">Rae</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer564535681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11782058645253450915">I'm pretty sick of saying the same thing...EVERY FREAKING ONE OF THESE BOOKS HAVE THE SAME FORMAT. Here's a summary of EVERY FREAKING BOOK IN THIS SERIES: <br/><br/>The heroine: an unsuspecting, blonde, beautiful, petite (except Circenn's wife), 20-something year old virgin has finally made a life for herself from her less than perfect upbringing. She can feel that her life's not perfect and there's something missing in it.<br/><br/>The hero: he's a six and a half foot, beautiful/handsome beyond belief, physically </span>
  <span id="freeText11782058645253450915" style="display:none">I'm pretty sick of saying the same thing...EVERY FREAKING ONE OF THESE BOOKS HAVE THE SAME FORMAT. Here's a summary of EVERY FREAKING BOOK IN THIS SERIES: <br /><br />The heroine: an unsuspecting, blonde, beautiful, petite (except Circenn's wife), 20-something year old virgin has finally made a life for herself from her less than perfect upbringing. She can feel that her life's not perfect and there's something missing in it.<br /><br />The hero: he's a six and a half foot, beautiful/handsome beyond belief, physically brawn, and more powerful than everyone around-alpha male. Let's not forget--he's also anatomically overly well endowed, with dark hair and dark eyes (except Daegus, who's eyes only turned dark when he used too much magic while he was possessed), and women swooned over him (the hero) everywhere he went. He is at the lowest point in his life.<br /><br />The two meet, fall in love and conquer some crisis that will forever change the world if they don't stop it. Most of the books are 300-350 pages long. They usually have their first kiss somewhere around chapter 10-13ish; first sex within the LAST 75 pages (then proceed to couple/tup every chance they could) of the book; some event will cause her to loose him (death, time travel, misunderstanding, etc,...) within the last 50 pages of the book; she's bereft by the lose and grieves, and finally they find out they love each other within the last 15 pages of the book.<br /><br />By this book, 'The Immortal Highlander' everyone from books 1-6 has had children.<br /><br />I'm happy that Ms. Moning is a successful author. I'm happy that her cookie-cutter format works for her and so many of her followers. For myself, once I complete the bundle (books 1-7) which I'm determined to get my money's worth from, I doubt I would read or recommend Ms. Moning's Series to anyone.<br /><br />Happy reading,<br /><br />Rae</span>
  <a data-text-id="11782058645253450915" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_128861467" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/128861467" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/128861467?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-karen-marie-moning">author-karen-marie-moning</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-historical-romance">genre-historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=the-hymen-club">the-hymen-club</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer128861467" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15863927671011511751">Stripped from his Fae powers and forced to live in the human world, Adam Black has never felt so vulnerable in his entire existence. With only the ability to sift in short distances and invisible to all humans and fae alike, his punishment from Aoibheal is one of pure torture. It isn’t until he realizes that only one other person can see him that he has some hope to become the immortal once again. <br/><br/>Gabrielle O’Callaghan is a woman who possesses a rare ability to see both realms: mortal and Faery.</span>
  <span id="freeText15863927671011511751" style="display:none">Stripped from his Fae powers and forced to live in the human world, Adam Black has never felt so vulnerable in his entire existence. With only the ability to sift in short distances and invisible to all humans and fae alike, his punishment from Aoibheal is one of pure torture. It isn’t until he realizes that only one other person can see him that he has some hope to become the immortal once again. <br /><br />Gabrielle O’Callaghan is a woman who possesses a rare ability to see both realms: mortal and Faery. Plagued with this burden her entire life, Gabby finds herself hating the Fae and even more, hating her undeniable attraction for them.<br /><br />When Adam seeks Gabby out to ask her to help him find his son Circenn in order to bring him back to face Aoibheal, sparks fly and the chemistry sizzles as Gabby tries to resist Adam’s charms. The Immortal Highlander is a fascinating, well-written story that questions if a Fae prince without a soul can give up his entire heart for a mere mortal.<br /><br />Moning crafts amazingly well-paced stories in this series, but I have to say that the Immortal Highlander may be my favourite of the bunch. Though Adam Black can be seen as the bad guy, there is just something so darkly alluring about the bad ones that you can’t help but love. Black is no exception. He is enchanting, compelling, passionate and downright sexy. <br /><br />Familiar faces are bought back into this book. The MacKelter twins, Drustan and Daegus and their wives Gwen and Chloe make appearances that make a reader like me grin from ear-to-ear. With such memorable characters with distinct personality traits and quirks, Moning makes me wish I were able to travel into their world and experience the magic myself.<br /><br />With one last Highlander book left for me to read, I am a little saddened to know that the end is near. I’ve fallen hard for all the books in the series. Bringing sexual tension in spades, Moning certainly knows how to do a romance right. I just hope that she’ll one day return to this time and bring us more highlander heroes to die for.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15863927671011511751" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
